***doceren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doceren.html>doceren</a> (45625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">doceō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doceren.html>doceren</a></strong>
</p>

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dof.html>dof</a> (31973)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a lang="odt">*dōf</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic <p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doctor.html>doctor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:doctor.html>doctor</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:person.html>person</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:who.html>who</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> attained <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> doctorate)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doctor.html>doctor</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:doctor.html>doctor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:teacher.html>teacher</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:instructor.html>instructor</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="id"><a href = vnd.unilang:dokter.html>dokter</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dolheid.html>dolheid</a> (107536)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dulheit</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dol.html>dol</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:crazy.html>crazy</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:mad.html>mad</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:insane.html>insane</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dolheid.html>dolheid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dolheid.html>dolheden</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dolheid.html>dolheidje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
